		trigger = {
			tag = GER
		}
	}
	desc = {

		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = lec.2.d.usa
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = lec.2.d.austria
		trigger = {
			tag = AUS
		}
	}

		text = lec.2.d.belgium
		trigger = {
			tag = BEL
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_LEC_shanghai_river
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = lec.2.a
		add_political_power = 25

			LEC_generic_open_door
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER

			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = lec.2.b

		add_ideas = LEC_USA_open_door

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = lec.2.c
		add_political_power = 25
		add_ideas = LEC_GER_open_door
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #A Legation Navy?
	id = lec.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lec.4" }
	title = lec.4.t
	desc = lec.4.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_battleship_kongo
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Of course!
		name = lec.4.a
		set_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		activate_mission = LEC_vote_timer
		country_event = {
			id = lec.6
			days = 15
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.5
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Legation navy? - Result
	id = lec.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lec.6" }
	title = lec.6.t
	desc = lec.6.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_battleship_kongo
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Approved!
		name = lec.6.a
		decrease_currency_reserve = yes
		country_event = {
			id = lec.8
			days = 30
		}
		set_country_flag = LEC_navy_approved
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_legation_navy_vote
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing

		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}

		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.28
				add_timed_idea = { idea = LEC_naval_building days = 25 }
			}
		}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
					check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > 0 }
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_COLLAPSE
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_TRIADS
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_TRIADS_JIANG
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_TRIADS_SEN
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_TRIADS_JINRONG
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_TRIADS_ZHANG
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_TRIADS_SHUNTIAN
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = lec.6.b
		add_political_power = -75
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_legation_navy_vote
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.27
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_COLLAPSE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_JIANG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_SEN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_JINRONG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_ZHANG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_SHUNTIAN
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = lec.7.a
		add_stability = -0.2
		custom_effect_tooltip = lec_black_monday
		hidden_effect = {
			decrease_currency_reserve = yes
		}
		decrease_currency_reserve = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_ideas = LEC_black_monday
	}
}

country_event = { #Vote on Russian Vote Restoration?
	id = lec.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lec.10" }
	title = lec.10.t
	desc = lec.10.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Of course!
		name = lec.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		activate_mission = LEC_vote_timer
		set_global_flag = LEC_russia_vote
		set_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.11
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = lec.12
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = lec.13
			days = 15
		}
	}
	option = {	#We don't need a vote...
		name = lec.10.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.14
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TRM = { 
					exists = yes 
				}
			}
			TRM = {
				country_event = {
					id = lec.109
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = lec.15
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Russian Vote - Result
	id = lec.13
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lec.13" }
	title = lec.13.t
	desc = lec.13.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Approved!
		name = lec.13.a
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_russia_vote
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = lec.15
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TRM = { 
					exists = yes 
				}
			}
			TRM = {
				country_event = {
					id = lec.109
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.28
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
				check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = lec.13.b
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_russia_vote
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = lec.16
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TRM = { 
					exists = yes 
				}
			}
			TRM = {
				country_event = {
					id = lec.109
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.27
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Vote on Sichuan aid?
	id = lec.20
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lec.20" }
	title = lec.20.t
	desc = lec.20.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_sichuan_map
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Of course!
		name = lec.20.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		activate_mission = LEC_vote_timer
		set_global_flag = LEC_sichuan_famine_vote

		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.21
			}
		}
		SZC = {
			country_event = {
				id = lec.22
			}
		}

			id = lec.23
			days = 15
		}
	}
	option = {	#Tough luck Sichuan, we don't like Chinese
		name = lec.20.b

			factor = 1

country_event = { #Sichuan Famine - Result
	id = lec.23
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lec.23" }
	title = lec.23.t
	desc = lec.23.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_sichuan_map
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Approved!
		name = lec.23.a
		decrease_currency_reserve = yes
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_sichuan_famine_vote
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		SZC = {
			country_event = {
				id = lec.25
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.28
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
					check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > 0 }
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_COLLAPSE
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_TRIADS
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_TRIADS_JIANG
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_TRIADS_SEN
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_TRIADS_JINRONG
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_TRIADS_ZHANG
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_TRIADS_SHUNTIAN
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = lec.23.b
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_sichuan_famine_vote
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		SZC = {
			country_event = {
				id = lec.26
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.27
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_COLLAPSE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_JIANG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_SEN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_JINRONG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_ZHANG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_SHUNTIAN
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = lec.36.t

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = legation_council_member
			has_country_flag = legation_council_vote
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { country_exists = LEC }
			AND = {
				LEC = {
					is_subject = yes
					NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { tag = GER }
					NOT = {
						var:LEC.overlord = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = QIE_german_influence_dynamic_modifier } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = LEC_dead_clumsy_coding
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }
	option = {	#ehhh whatever
		name = lec.36.a
		add_political_power = -5
		set_country_flag = LEC_dead_clumsy_coding
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { global.LEC_voters = ROOT } }
			remove_from_array = { global.LEC_voters = ROOT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = legation_council_member }
			clr_country_flag = legation_council_member
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = legation_council_vote }
			clr_country_flag = legation_council_vote
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_generic_open_door }
			remove_ideas = { LEC_generic_open_door }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_better_open_door }
			remove_ideas = { LEC_better_open_door }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_USA_open_door }
			remove_ideas = { LEC_USA_open_door }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_GER_open_door }
			remove_ideas = { LEC_GER_open_door }
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_LEC_shanghai_river
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#I don't care
		name = lec.43.a
		add_political_power = -1
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { global.LEC_voters = BEL } }
			remove_from_array = { global.LEC_voters = BEL }
		}
		clr_country_flag = legation_council_vote
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_generic_open_door }
			remove_ideas = { LEC_generic_open_door }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_better_open_door }
			remove_ideas = { LEC_better_open_door }
		}
		remove_opinion_modifier = { target = LEC modifier = LEC_member }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = LEC modifier = LEC_removed_council }
		LEC = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = BEL modifier = LEC_member }
		}
		ROOT = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = LEC
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = LEC
				relation = military_access
				active = no
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {

				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = no
			}

	title = lec.47.t

	option = {	#They're kicked out
		name = lec.47.a

			country_event = {
				id = lec.43
				days = 1
			}
		}
		QIE = {
			country_event = {
				id = lec.50
				days = 5
			}
		}
		FNG = {
			country_event = {
				id = lec.50
				days = 5
			}
		}
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_belgium_vote
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.28
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
				check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = lec.47.b
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_belgium_vote
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.27
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

			}

			}
		}

					}

				}
			}
		}
	}

		}

					id = lec.103
				}

		}

				}

			}

				country_event = {
					id = lec.117
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.27
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Legation Cities gets concessions
	id = lec.127
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lec.127 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = lec.127.t
	desc = lec.127.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	trigger = {
		any_owned_state = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = LEC
				is_possible_legation_cities_state = yes
			}
			is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			if = {

			}
		}
	}

		name = lec.127.a

			base = 5
		}

			limit = {
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				OR = {
					is_core_of = LEC
					is_possible_legation_cities_state = yes
					AND = {
						is_mainland_china = yes
						LEC = { has_cosmetic_tag = LEC_china }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { tag = JAP } }
					NOT = { has_variable = ambition_area_@ROOT }
				}
			}
			remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
			LEC = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		LEC = { country_event = lec.128 }
	}
	option = {	# no
		name = lec.127.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		LEC = {
			country_event = { id = lec.129 days = 1 }
		}
	}

		}

		trigger = {

				has_government = market_liberal
				has_government = paternal_autocrat

		}

		}
		OR = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_government = market_liberal

			has_government = national_populist
		}

	option = {	#Uh...

				has_government = social_conservative

		add_political_power = -25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.5
		}
	}
	option = {	#Now we're screwed
		name = lec.130.b
		trigger = {
			has_government = national_populist
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.1
		decrease_currency_reserve = yes
		country_event = { id = lec.131 days = 5 }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.5
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_supply_lines_idea }
			remove_ideas = LEC_supply_lines_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_TMKKD_idea }
			remove_ideas = LEC_TMKKD_idea
		}
	}
	option = {	#Serves them right!
		name = lec.100.b
		trigger = {
			has_government = paternal_autocrat
		}
		add_political_power = 5
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -1
		}
	}
}

	id = lec.131
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lec.131 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

	trigger = {
		has_war = no
		NOT = { 
		has_country_flag = JAP_was_in_sphere
		has_country_flag = LEC_Triad_Power
		has_country_flag = LEC_Shuntian_Power	
		has_country_leader = { name = "Francis Arthur Sutton" ruling_only = yes }		
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#The Americans are clearly the best option
		name = lec.131.a
		trigger = {
			market_liberal > 0.2
			NOT = { country_exists = CSA }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { LEC_help_yank_desire = party_popularity@market_liberal }
				multiply_temp_variable = { LEC_help_yank_desire = 100 }
				add = LEC_help_yank_desire
				always = yes
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		lec_american_rise = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = legation_council_member
						has_country_flag = legation_council_vote
					}
				}
				country_event = lec.132
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Anglos
		name = lec.131.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = LEC_AST_governor
			social_conservative > 0.2
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0.9
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { LEC_help_britain_desire = party_popularity@social_conservative }
				multiply_temp_variable = { LEC_help_britain_desire = 100 }
				add = LEC_help_britain_desire
				always = yes
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		lec_british_rise = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = legation_council_member
						has_country_flag = legation_council_vote
					}
				}
				country_event = lec.133
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Germans
		name = lec.131.c
		trigger = {
			GER = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				surrender_progress < 0.2
			}
			paternal_autocrat > 0.2
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0.9
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { LEC_help_germany_desire = party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
				multiply_temp_variable = { LEC_help_germany_desire = 100 }
				add = LEC_help_germany_desire
				always = yes
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		lec_german_rise = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = legation_council_member
						has_country_flag = legation_council_vote
					}
				}
				country_event = lec.134
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Just give up to the Chinese
		name = lec.131.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		trigger = {
			var:613.owner = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = LEC_surrender_to_china
		set_country_flag = LEC_dead_to_china
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = legation_council_member
					has_country_flag = legation_council_vote
				}
			}
			country_event = lec.136
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_guaranteed = LEC
					has_non_aggression_pact_with = LEC
					has_military_access_to = LEC
					gives_military_access_to = LEC
				}
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = no
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = military_access
				active = no
			}
			LEC = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = PREV
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			var:613.owner = {
				country_event = { id = lec.135 days = 1 }
			}
			var:1066.owner = { country_event = lec.62 }
			var:1068.owner = { country_event = lec.64 }
			var:1012.owner = { country_event = lec.66 }
			var:608.owner = { country_event = lec.68 }
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 326 }
				var:593.owner = { country_event = lec.70 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 729 }
				var:593.owner = { country_event = lec.99 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#We are China now!
		name = lec.131.f

		}

			base = 1000

		name = lec.140.a

		set_country_flag = cannot_have_extensive_conscription
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes

		clr_global_flag = LEC_conscription_vote
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		add_ideas = limited_conscription

			array = global.LEC_voters
			clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
			country_event = lec.141
		}

		trigger = {
			check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
			check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > 0 }
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = lec.140.b
		add_political_power = -75
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_conscription_vote
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
			country_event = lec.27
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Bailout the DAB? - Result
	id = lecshorting.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lecshorting.4" }
	title = lecshorting.4.t
	desc = lecshorting.4.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_NOR_black_monday_2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Approved!
		name = lecshorting.4.a
		decrease_currency_reserve = yes
		country_event = {
			id = lecshorting.6
			days = 4
		}
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_DAB_bailout_question
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.28
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
					check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > 0 }
				}
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_COLLAPSE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_JIANG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_SEN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_JINRONG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_ZHANG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_SHUNTIAN
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = lecshorting.4.b
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				country_event = {
					id = lecshorting.5
					days = 7
				}
			}
			50 = {
				country_event = {
					id = lecshorting.6
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_DAB_bailout_question
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.LEC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = lec.28
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_COLLAPSE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_JIANG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_SEN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_JINRONG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_ZHANG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_TRIADS_SHUNTIAN
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Australia goes syndie/AFM and loses their China stuff
	id = lecbrits.28
	title = lecbrits.28.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_LEC_shanghai_river

	desc = {
		text = lecbrits.28.d.govt
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_socialist_government = yes
				AND = {
					tag = AST
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = lecbrits.28.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_socialist_government = yes
				AND = {
					tag = AST
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = LEC
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = AST_hong_kong
			has_country_flag = legation_council_member
			has_country_flag = legation_council_vote
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lecbrits.28"
		if = {
			limit = {
				GBR = {
					exists = yes
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			GBR = { save_global_event_target_as = LEC_has_british_vote }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				CAN = {
					exists = yes
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			CAN = { save_global_event_target_as = LEC_has_british_vote }
		}
		else = {
			clear_global_event_target = LEC_has_british_vote
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lecbrits.28.a
		trigger = { has_event_target = LEC_has_british_vote }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = AST_hong_kong }
			clr_country_flag = AST_hong_kong
			event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = { set_country_flag = AST_hong_kong }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = legation_council_member }
			clr_country_flag = legation_council_member
			event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = { set_country_flag = legation_council_member }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = legation_council_vote }
			clr_country_flag = legation_council_vote
			event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = { set_country_flag = legation_council_vote }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_generic_open_door }
			remove_ideas = { LEC_generic_open_door }
			event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = { add_ideas = LEC_generic_open_door }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_better_open_door }
			remove_ideas = { LEC_better_open_door }
			event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = { add_ideas = LEC_better_open_door }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { global.LEC_voters = ROOT } }
			remove_from_array = { global.LEC_voters = ROOT }
			add_to_array = { global.LEC_voters = event_target:LEC_has_british_vote }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_opinion_modifier = LEC_member }
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = LEC modifier = LEC_member }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { LEC = { is_guaranteed_by = ROOT } }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = LEC
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { LEC = { gives_military_access_to = ROOT } }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = LEC
				relation = military_access
				active = no
			}
		}
		LEC = {
			country_event = lecbrits.26
		}
		event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = {
			country_event = lecbrits.29
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = lecbrits.28.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_event_target = LEC_has_british_vote } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = AST_hong_kong }
			clr_country_flag = AST_hong_kong
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = legation_council_member }
			clr_country_flag = legation_council_member
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = legation_council_vote }
			clr_country_flag = legation_council_vote
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_generic_open_door }
			remove_ideas = { LEC_generic_open_door }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_better_open_door }
			remove_ideas = { LEC_better_open_door }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { global.LEC_voters = ROOT } }
			remove_from_array = { global.LEC_voters = ROOT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_opinion_modifier = LEC_member }
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = LEC modifier = LEC_member }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { LEC = { is_guaranteed_by = ROOT } }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = LEC
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { LEC = { gives_military_access_to = ROOT } }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = LEC
				relation = military_access
				active = no
			}
		}
		LEC = {
			country_event = lecbrits.26
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #British Vote - Result
	id = lecbrits.44
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event lecbrits.44" }
	title = lecbrits.44.t
	desc = lecbrits.44.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#Approved!
		name = lecbrits.44.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
			check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > 0 }
		}
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_britain_vote
		set_country_flag = LEC_brits_vote
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = {
			country_event = {
				id = lecbrits.46
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.LEC_voters
				THIS = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time }
						clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					country_event = lec.28
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = lecbrits.44.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.legations_yes_votes > global.legations_no_votes }
			}
		}
		clear_variable = global.legations_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.legations_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = LEC_britain_vote
		clr_global_flag = legation_vote_ongoing
		event_target:LEC_has_british_vote = { country_event = lecbrits.47 }
		hidden_effect = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.LEC_voters
				THIS = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time }
						clr_country_flag = LEC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					country_event = lec.27
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = lecbrits.46.a
		add_political_power = 25
		add_to_array = { global.LEC_voters = ROOT }
		set_country_flag = legation_council_vote
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = LEC_generic_open_door }
			}
			add_ideas = {
				LEC_generic_open_door
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = LEC_member }
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = LEC modifier = LEC_member }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LEC = { NOT = { is_guaranteed_by = ROOT } }
			}
			give_guarantee = LEC
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LEC = { NOT = { gives_military_access_to = ROOT } }
			}
			LEC = {
				give_military_access = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

						has_country_flag = legation_council_vote
					}
				}

					id = lecyankded.15
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = LEC_new_high_commissioner
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_populist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		lec_japanese_rise = yes
	}
	option = {	#Krauts it is
		name = lecyankded.13.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				paternal_autocrat > 0.18
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_GER
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { LEC_help_germany_desire = party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
				multiply_temp_variable = { LEC_help_germany_desire = 100 }
				add = LEC_help_germany_desire
				always = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_GER
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {

				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = legation_council_member
						has_country_flag = legation_council_vote
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = lecyankded.16
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = LEC_new_high_commissioner
		LEC_exile_koreshige_inuzuka = yes
		LEC_exile_francis_wogan_festing = yes
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		lec_german_rise = yes
	}
	option = {	#Anglos
		name = lecyankded.13.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = LEC_AST_governor
					social_conservative > 0.18
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_UK
				}
			}
		}

			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_UK
				}

			AND = {

			}
		}
	}

		name = lecyankded.26.b

		clear_variable = global.legations_no_votes

				}

					id = lecyankded.28
				}
			}
		}
		if = {

				TEX = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			TEX = {
				country_event = {
					id = lecyankded.28
				}
			}
		}

					exists = yes

				}
			}
		}

					exists = yes
				}
			}

				}
			}
		}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	# Agree
		name = lectianjap.1.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LEC_path
					option = LEC_JAP
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_GER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_USA
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LEC_path
						option = LEC_UK
					}
				}
			}
		}

		add_political_power = -20

		LEC = {
			lec_japanese_rise = yes
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = lectianjap.18
					days = 2
				}
			}

			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.LEC_voters
				THIS = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { tag = JAP }
						}
						country_event = {
							id = lectianjap.19
							days = 2
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	# Refuse
		name = lectianjap.1.b

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = lectianjap.20
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Trigger event in legation council members that dividends will stop. Triggered by triad1 focus
country_event = {
	id = legcities.59
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event legcities.59"}
	title = legcities.59.t
	desc = legcities.59.d
	picture = profits

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = legcities.59.a
		remove_ideas = LEC_paying_out
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = legation_council_member
					has_country_flag = legation_council_vote
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = legcities.60
				days = 5
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				remove_ideas = LEC_generic_open_door
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					target = LEC modifier = LEC_member
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = LEC
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = LEC
						relation = guarantee
						active = no
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = LEC
						relation = military_access
						active = no
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				LEC = {
					country_event = {
						id = legcities.62
						days = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Inform council members that LEC has stopped paying dividends, give option for intervention.
country_event = {
	id = legcities.60
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event legcities.60"}
	title = legcities.60.t
	desc = {
		text = legcities.60.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = LEC_USA_open_door
				has_idea = LEC_GER_open_door
				has_idea = LEC_generic_open_door
				has_idea = LEC_better_open_door
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = legcities.60.no_proff
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = LEC_USA_open_door
				has_idea = LEC_GER_open_door
				has_idea = LEC_generic_open_door
				has_idea = LEC_better_open_door
			}
		}
	}
	picture = profits

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = triads_seize_LEC_profits
		remove_ideas = LEC_legation_cities_open_door
		}
	}

	# Nothing we can do
	option = {
		name = legcities.60.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 200
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_USA_open_door }
			remove_ideas = LEC_USA_open_door
			set_country_flag = had_full_proff_leg_cities
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_GER_open_door }
			remove_ideas = LEC_GER_open_door
			set_country_flag = had_full_proff_leg_cities
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_better_open_door }
			remove_ideas = LEC_better_open_door
			set_country_flag = had_full_proff_leg_cities
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = LEC_generic_open_door }
			remove_ideas = LEC_generic_open_door
			set_country_flag = had_minor_proff_leg_cities
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = LEC }
			if = {
				limit = { has_opinion_modifier = LEC_member }
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = LEC modifier = LEC_member }
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = LEC modifier = INVEST_SEIZED }
			if = {
				limit = { LEC = { is_guaranteed_by = ROOT } }
				diplomatic_relation = { country = LEC relation = guarantee active = no }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { LEC = { gives_military_access_to = ROOT } }
				diplomatic_relation = { country = LEC relation = military_access active = no }
			}
		}
	}

	#Time for an intervention
	option = {
		name = legcities.60.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
				LEC = { is_ai = no }
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = LEC_USA_open_door
			}
			remove_ideas = LEC_USA_open_door
			set_country_flag = had_full_proff_leg_cities
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = LEC_GER_open_door
			}
			remove_ideas = LEC_GER_open_door
			set_country_flag = had_full_proff_leg_cities
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = LEC_better_open_door
			}
			remove_ideas = LEC_better_open_door
			set_country_flag = had_full_proff_leg_cities
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = LEC_generic_open_door
			}
			remove_ideas = LEC_generic_open_door
			set_country_flag = had_minor_proff_leg_cities
		}
		LEC = {
			set_country_flag = LEC_foreign_intervention_planned
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_major = yes
					OR = {
						has_war = no
						NOT = {
							any_enemy_country = {
								is_major = yes
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
				tag = JAP
			}
		}

		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = LEC
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = LEC
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_opinion_modifier = LEC_member
				}
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					target = LEC modifier = LEC_member
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = LEC
				modifier = INVEST_SEIZED
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = LEC
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = LEC
				relation = military_access
				active = no
			}
			LEC = {
				country_event = {
					id = legcities.61
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Jiang/Mao
	id = legcities.150
	title = legcities.150.t
	desc = legcities.150.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_LEC_jiang_mao
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
	tag = LEC
	LEC = { is_ai = no }
	has_completed_focus = LEC_madame_jiang_qing_steals_show
	OR = {
	CHI = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mao Zedong" } }

		}
	}

					}
				add_core_of = LEC
			}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = CHI
			}
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		MON = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mao Zedong" } }
		}
		every_state = {
                limit = {
					is_core_of = MON
					}
				add_core_of = LEC
			}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = MON
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = LEC_jiang_mao
	}
	option = {
		name = legcities.150.b
		add_political_power = -100
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = LEC_Mao_Zedong_hog_tot
		if = {
		limit = {
		CHI = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mao Zedong" } }
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = CHI
			transfer_troops = yes
			}
			CHI = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = LEC
				}
			}
		CHI = { transfer_technology = yes }
		every_state = {
                limit = {
					is_core_of = CHI
					}
				add_core_of = LEC
			}
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		MON = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mao Zedong" } }
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = MON
			transfer_troops = yes
			}
			MON = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = LEC
				}
			}
		MON = { transfer_technology = yes }
		every_state = {
                limit = {
					is_core_of = MON
					}
				add_core_of = LEC
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = LEC_jiang_mao
	}
